##include <stdio.h>
int main ()
{
int n,x,y;
int s;
scanf("%d%d%d",&n,&x,&y);
if (y%x==0&&y/x<=n){
s=n-(y/x);
printf("%d",s);
}

s=n-1-(y/x);
printf("%d",s);
}
else {
s=0;
printf("%d",s);
}
return 0;
}
